                     
   RTU_RecStruct √Ω√ø       ‚Ä¢  It is Record table which holds records that define Modbus RTU query. Record table is an ARRAY OF
structure of type RTU_RecStruct. Members of the record are as shown below
GR			BYTE		Helps in grouping queries. depending on value of ‚ÄòGrSel‚Äô in auto mode
FNC		BYTE		Defines function code as per Modbus RTU protocol as below
						FNC		Function
						  1			Read coil status
						  2			Read input status
						  3			Read holding register
						  4			Read input register
						  5			Force single coil
						  6			Preset single register
						  15	       Force multiple coils
						  16	       Force multiple registers
SNO		BYTE		Holds target Modbus station number (1 to 247). 0  means broadcast command.                                 
LDT		RTU_TT    This is enumerated variable of type RTU_TT that defines memory type as I, Q and M and refers to ‚ÄòLAdr‚Äô and ‚ÄòRAdr‚Äô
														   				   Enum	  Value		      Description
																			 I			0			Input area
																			Q			1			Output area
																			M			2			Marker area
LAdr		 WORD	Holds start address of Master PLC memory (defined by LDT)
													-where read data (from slave) is stored.
													-where write data (to slave) is stored
RAdr		 WORD	Holds memory address (holding register, coil, etc) in target Modbus RTU slave device. 
DLen		 BYTE		Holds number of addresses to read or write. Start address is defined by RAdr / LAdr.

In the example, the variable RecTable with 2 records is declared with following typical initialisation:
Record : array [0.. 1] of RecStruct :=
	(Gr:=1,		FNC:=3,	SNO:=1,	LDT:=M,	LAdr:=100,		RAdr:=0,	DLen:=16),
	(Gr:=1,		FNC:=16,	SNO:=1,	LDT:=M,	LAdr:=200,		RAdr:=50,	DLen:=16);
	Record0 defines query to Read holding registers which reads 16 registers (from 40000) and stores at %MW100 onward
	Record1 defines query to  Write muliple registers which writes 16 registers data from %MW200 to 40025 onwards	        √ªO  ‚Ç¨   √ø√ø√ø√ø        	   RTU_SLAVE     +   	   OpenPort1                     OpenPort   √Ω√ø              Receive                 ReceiveByte   √Ω√ø           	   STN_Match             √Ω√ø              TX                RTU_ComBuff   √Ω√ø           Local TX-Buffer for processing   RX                RTU_ComBuff   √Ω√ø             Local RX-Buffer for processing    FNC            √Ω√ø!              ComRecd             √Ω√ø"              Answered             √Ω√ø#

										Bit 0 : Becomes TRUE, if port is opened successfully with valid station number
	    									Bit 1 : Becomes TRUE, in case of checksum error in any previous query.

										Bit 0 : Becomes TRUE, if port is opened successfully with valid station number
	    									Bit 1 : Becomes TRUE, in case of checksum error in any previous query.
	    									Bit 2 : Becomes TRUE, if timeout is observed in reception of any previous query as well as transmission of any previous response due to any reason.
	    									Bit 6 : Becomes TRUE, in case of parity error in received byte.
	    									Bit 7 : Becomes TRUE, in case of frame error in received byte   Replies           √Ω√ø       $   Holds number of successful replies     ErrCount           √Ω√ø       %   Increments by 1 if
										1. Timeout in reception or transmission
										2. Checksum mismatch
										3. Any intermittant byte received is SOF
    										4. Any byte recived has frame/parity error
    										5. Querry contains address beyond supported range of a slave PLC       COMSET   
              
   RTU_ComSet √Ω√ø       √Ç     Define a variable e.g. "ComSet2 : RTU_ComSet;"
									    Default parameters are Comset=9600, Odd, 8, 1,

					IF sys.sdbs[j].limits.ls_sogu = 0 THEN												(*Check Plat on EG*)
						Flag_1:=TRUE;																	(*Flag for Task I(9)*)
						j:=j+1;
					ELSE
						IF sys.sdbs[j].limits.ls_sogo = 1 THEN										(*Check if called plat is on OG, if not ,move up*)
							sys.sdbs[j].ops.ogup:=TRUE;
						ELSE
							sys.sdbs[j].ops.ogup:=FALSE;
							j:=j+1;
						END_IF
					END_IF
				ELSE
					IF sys.sdbs[j].limits.ls_sogo = 1 THEN										(*Check if called plat is on OG, if not, move up*)
						sys.sdbs[j].ops.ogup:=TRUE;
					ELSE
						sys.sdbs[j].ops.ogup:=FALSE;
						j:=j+1;
					END_IF
				END_IF

							sys.sdbs[j].ops.ogup:=TRUE;

					END_IF

			ELSE
				Task:=11;																(*Task L (11)*)
			END_IF
		END_IF

				IF sys.sdbs[j].limits.ls_sugo = 0 THEN												(*Check Plat on EG*)
					Flag_1:=TRUE;																	(*Flag for Task I(9)*)
					j:=j+1;

						IF sys.sdbs[j].limits.ls_sugo=1 THEN								(*Move UG up and then down*)

						END_IF

									IF j>End_SDB THEN
										Task:=9;
										begin:=FALSE;
									END_IF
								END_IF
							ELSE
								sys.sdbs[j].ops.ugup:=FALSE;
								sys.sdbs[j].ops.ugdn:=TRUE;
							END_IF
					ELSE
							sys.sdbs[j].ops.ugup:=FALSE;
							sys.sdbs[j].ops.ugdn:=FALSE;
							j:=j+1;
					END_IF
					IF j>=End_SDB AND Flag_1=FALSE THEN
						Flag_2:=TRUE;																	(*Flag for Task E (5) *)
					END_IF
				END_IF

				IF Called_plat_typ=3 THEN															(*Called platform is OG*)
						IF sys.sdbs[j].limits.ls_sugu = 1 THEN									      (*Check if called plat is on UG, if not move down*)
							IF sys.sdbs[j].limits.ls_sugo=1 THEN									(*Move UG up and then down*)
								IF sys.sdbs[j].limits.ls_seg=1 AND sys.sdbs[j].limits.ls_sogu=1 THEN
									Counter3:=0;
									FOR l:=Start_SDB TO End_SDB BY 1 DO
											IF sys.sdbs[l].limits.ls_seg=1 THEN
												Counter3:=Counter3+1;
											END_IF
									END_FOR
									IF sys.sdbs[j].ops.ugdn=FALSE THEN
										IF Counter3>1 THEN
											bER150:=TRUE;						(*EG enable error*)
											Task:=9;
											begin:=FALSE;
											Counter3:=0;
										ELSE
											sys.sdbs[j].ops.ugup:=TRUE;
										END_IF
									END_IF
								ELSE
								(*	Task:=9;
									begin:=FALSE;*)
									j:=j+1;
									IF j>End_SDB THEN
										Task:=9;
										begin:=FALSE;
									END_IF
								END_IF
							ELSE
								sys.sdbs[j].ops.ugup:=FALSE;
								sys.sdbs[j].ops.ugdn:=TRUE;
							END_IF
						ELSE
							sys.sdbs[j].ops.ugup:=FALSE;
							sys.sdbs[j].ops.ugdn:=FALSE;
							j:=j+1;
							IF Called_SDB_no=Start_SDB AND Called_SDB_no<>End_SDB  THEN
								Flag_3:=TRUE;
							END_IF
							IF Called_SDB_no=End_SDB AND Called_SDB_no<>Start_SDB THEN
								Flag_4:=TRUE;
							END_IF
							IF Called_SDB_no<>Start_SDB AND Called_SDB_no<>End_SDB THEN
								Flag_5:=TRUE;
							END_IF
							IF Called_SDB_no=Start_SDB AND Called_SDB_no=End_SDB THEN
								Flag_6:=TRUE;
							END_IF
						END_IF
				END_IF
			END_IF
		ELSE																							(*Current platform is not called platfrom*)
			IF  sys.sdbs[j].limits.ls_sugu = 1 THEN													(*Check UG and move down one by one*)
				IF sys.sdbs[j].limits.ls_sugo=1 THEN												(*Move UG up and then down*)
					IF sys.sdbs[j].limits.ls_seg=1 AND sys.sdbs[j].limits.ls_sogu=1 THEN
						Counter4:=0;
						FOR l:=Start_SDB TO End_SDB BY 1 DO
								IF sys.sdbs[l].limits.ls_seg=1 THEN
									Counter4:=Counter4+1;
								END_IF
						END_FOR
						IF sys.sdbs[j].ops.ugdn=FALSE THEN
							IF Counter4>1 THEN
								bER150:=TRUE;						(*EG enable error*)
								Task:=9;
								begin:=FALSE;
								Counter4:=0;
							ELSE
								sys.sdbs[j].ops.ugup:=TRUE;
							END_IF
						END_IF
					ELSE

						begin:=FALSE;*)
						j:=j+1;
						IF j>End_SDB THEN
							Task:=9;
							begin:=FALSE;
						END_IF
					END_IF
				ELSE
					sys.sdbs[j].ops.ugup:=FALSE;
					IF k<>j OR Called_plat_typ<>2 THEN
						sys.sdbs[j].ops.ugdn:=TRUE;
					ELSIF k=j AND Called_plat_typ = 2 THEN
						sys.sdbs[j].ops.ugdn:=FALSE;
						Plat_on_EG_11:=TRUE;
						Flag_1:=TRUE;
						j:=j+1;
					END_IF
				END_IF
			ELSE
				sys.sdbs[j].ops.ugdn:=FALSE;
				sys.sdbs[j].ops.ugup:=FALSE;
				j:=j+1;
				IF j>=End_SDB AND Flag_1=FALSE AND Called_plat_typ=2 THEN
					Flag_2:=TRUE;																	(*Flag for Task E (5) *)
				END_IF
			END_IF
		END_IF

			j:=Start_SDB;
			begin:=FALSE;
			IF Flag_1= TRUE THEN
				Task:=9;																(*Task I (9)*)
				Flag_1:= FALSE;
				begin:=FALSE;
			END_IF

				Task:=5;																(*Task E (5)*)
				Flag_2:= FALSE;
			END_IF

				Task:=6;																(*Task F (6)*)
				Flag_3:=FALSE;
			END_IF

				Task:=3;																(*Task C (3)*)
				Flag_4:=FALSE;
			END_IF

			END_IF

	END_IF

		begin:=FALSE;
	END_IF

				sys.sdbs[j].ops.ogup:=TRUE;									(*OG UP*)
				Tdelay(IN:=TRUE);
			ELSE

				IF(flag34=FALSE) THEN
					FOR L:=Start_SDB TO End_SDB BY 1 DO
						IF sys.sdbs[L].limits.ls_seg = 1 THEN				(*NC & NO contact*)
						counter:=counter + 1;
						END_IF
					END_FOR
				END_IF
				IF counter <> 1THEN

					ELSE
						sys.sdbs[j].ops.ogdn:=FALSE;								(* OG DOWN False *)
						sys.sdbs[j].ops.ogup:=FALSE;								(* OG UP False *)

						begin:=FALSE;
						Task:=9;
					END_IF
				END_IF
			END_IF
		ELSE

				sys.sdbs[j].ops.ogdn:=FALSE;								(* OG DOWN False *)
				sys.sdbs[j].ops.ogup:=FALSE;								(* OG UP False *)
			END_IF

			begin:=FALSE;
			Tdelay(IN:=FALSE);

	END_IF

				ELSE
					sys.sdbs[j].ops.ogdn:=FALSE;									(* OG DOWN False *)
					sys.sdbs[j].ops.ogup:=FALSE;									(* OG UP False *)
					Tdelay(IN:=FALSE);												(*Stop Timer*)
					begin:=FALSE;
					Task:=9;
				END_IF
			END_IF
		ELSE
			(*Return j and update error no*)
			Task:=9;
			begin:=FALSE;
			Tdelay(IN:=FALSE);
		END_IF
	END_IF
ELSE
	IF bL_ERROR=1 OR bTOP_ERR=1  THEN
		Task:=9;
		Tdelay(IN:=FALSE);
		begin:=FALSE;
	END_IF
END_IF               √§   ,   ¬∫‚Äû                  Task_9 ≈†K√∂\	≈†K√∂\      √ç√ç√ç√ç√ç√ç√ç√ç        √é   PROGRAM Task_9							(*Task_9(I) All output OFF*)

						Flag_EG_called:=FALSE;
					END_IF

				ELSE

					IF TOn1.Q=TRUE THEN
						Flag1:=FALSE;
						TOn1(IN:=Flag1);
					END_IF

						P_NO:=0;
						Flag_EG_called:=FALSE;

						Called_SDB_no:=0;
						Flag_EGSP1:=FALSE;
						Flag_EGSP2:=FALSE;
						Flag_EGSP3:=FALSE;
						Flag_EGSP4:=FALSE;
						Flag_EGSP5:=FALSE;
						Flag_EGSP6:=FALSE;
						(*bbER150:=FALSE;*)
						Task:=0;
						begin:=FALSE;
					END_IF(*Flag1*)
				END_IF
			END_IF
	END_IF(*begin*)
